Though Shri Gurudev behaved like an ordinary man in this world, his every action was purposeful, and the purpose was purely spiritual one. Without a shred of doubt he read the thought in my mind and gave proper answer to me. This is not possible for an ordinary Yogi. It is only those, who have identified themselves with universal consciousness, who can read correctly the minds of others and give proper answers. This is an incident which has left an indelible impression on my mind of the grandeur of Shri Gurudev's spiritual height. I have related the same as briefly as I could. Readers are free to draw their conclusions. I can say this much that I have faithfully recorded the event though it took place many years back, may be in 1950-51.

(20)

**Gurudeo as I saw Him**

*By : Prof. P. M. Upadhye*

It is said that a man gets a new-birth in spiritual life after his mere contact with the Guru and this is what has happened in my case in the real sense of the term. It was the blessed day, twenty four years ago, when I saw Gurudeo for the first time in life. I was having dark night or my soul hankering after the day-light and lo, at once, a new divine light in the form of Gurudeo flashed forth before me, it was not the heat but it was the moon-light soothing my soul by the presence of the nectar-like rays of the moon in the form of Gurudeo. More wonderful thing that I experienced was that I surrendered myself to Him and his divine touch and divine look filled my entire body and I lost myself for a minute. I still remember this inexpressible state of my mind in his presence. He did not say anything to me, but everything that I needed to begin *Śādhakāvasthā* was conveyed to me. It was strength to me to learn the spiritual life and I have been trying in my humble way to follow it.

This is how I saw Gurudeo twenty four years ago. After

my first visit to Him, I was once again attracted towards him and I used to meet him often. In the meetings he spoke few words, Words of wisdom, full of divine life and it could electrify any layman near him. I was such a fortunate soul near him. He used to explain the source of vedanta sutras or a Rgvedic hymn on Pāsan. I could hardly understand him because he used to speak indirectly about his divine life through the words therein. It was beyond my reach because I was far away from such life. I was a man of flesh and blood. He was a superman, a real Sadguru who inspired the Sādhakas like me for spiritual life and we know that Gurudet spent his whole life for this mission and he lived for this Divine mission, till he breathed his last.

Whenever I saw Him, I always noticed divine light around him. I also thought that I was as if meeting *Yājnavalkya* of the Upanisadic times or I was meeting saint Ekanatha. All the divine qualities were seen in Him and I looked upon him as one such *Vibhuti* as described in the 10th chapter of the *Gīrā*.

He was the embodiment of knowledge and faith to us. All the characteristics of an ideal *bhakta* or a teacher as described in ancient literature were also found in Him. His love was grace. his speech was knowledge, his touch was divine, his sight was nectar-like rays. This was the feeling in my heart. Whenever I remember Him and his words, I am still thrilled. Nimbal, the very spiritual seat of his divine life, is a great solace to many sādhakas like me and I pray to Him to shower His grace on all the sādhakas to lead the spiritual life. May He take us from darkness to light ! May He take us from death to immortality !

(21)

**Gurudev As I Saw Him**

( *G. V. Tulapule* )

( *A free English rendering by P.-f. D. G. Kulkarni, M. A. of the original Marathi article from Mr. G. V. Tulpule* )

It was in the year 1908 that I was first acquainted with Gurudev. I had then joined the Deccan College, Poona and he was a Fellow there, teaching Sanskrit Poetry to our Class. I looked upon him then mostly in my capacity as one interested in moral and spiritual Philosophy. But when I was initiated by Shri Bhausaheb Maharaj in 1911, I began to regard him in my capacity as a *Sādhak*, and began to regard him as an ideal *Sādhak*. My fortunate contact with him went on ripening into a close intimacy right upto his demise in 1957. During this long period of nearly fifty years, I had the unique good fortune of studying the various facets of rich, brilliant, pure and purifying personality. I give below some of my reminiscences of Gurudev's life and personality :-

a) His wonderful confidence and conviction regarding his thoughts as seen in his casual conversation :-

i) In the year 1914, I went to see him at the Deccan

College, Pune, He had to go out for a few minutes and so he opened Dnaneshwari and asked me to read it till he returned The page contained the following verse from the commentary on B. G. 9/2.

सुखाच्या पाऊटी । येईजे जयाचिये भेटी ।
भेटल्या कीर मिठी । सुखातेही पडे ॥

The main idea in it is that a *Sādhak* climbs the path of God-realization by the steps of spiritual bliss and finally he becomes one with the bliss itself. I brought this to the notice of Gurudev and asked, " Is there a degree of rising spiritual bliss even in the *Sādhak* State ? ". He very gently said " Yes, Ganpatrao. If it were not so, how would it be possible to climb this difficult path of God-realisation ? " Later on, in due course I read his books and was convinced that spiritual bliss was the Central principle of the Science of God-realisation.

ii) During his stay at Nimbal, I once asked, " How is one to know that his spiritual *Sādhana* has reached perfection? " In reply to my question Gurudev immediately quoted the following verses from Dasabodha -

“ पापाची खंडना झाली । जन्मयातना चुकली । ऐसी स्वयं प्रचीति आली । म्हणजे वरे ॥ मुख्य देवासी ओळखिले । मी कोण हें जाणलें । आत्मनिवेदन झालें । म्हणजे वरे ॥ हें व्रम्हांड कोठोनि आलें । कासयाचे उभारिले । मुख्य कर्त्यासि ओळखिलें । म्हणजे वरे ॥

In these lines we are told that God is the only Reality, the Self and universe are illusory. One must know this by personal experience and this experience annihilates all Sin and suffering and becomes a mark of perfection of spiritual life. Both these doctrines are clearly reflected in Gurudev's writings.

iii) When I was with him at Allahabad in 1936, I asked him, "We read and hear that there are different ways to God-realisation such as Karma, Jnana, Bhakti and Dhyana. Are there really such different ways ? OR, is there only the one way, that of *Nāmasmarana*, as practised by us ?". In reply to my question, Gurudev lifted up his hands and bringing them down as a sign of his conviction ( to carry conviction ) he said,

" There is no other path to attain God - realisation." He further explained that *Nāmasmarana* - and Self-realisation attained through it-is the only way of God-Realisation. There is none other. In his books, especially the one on Karnatak mysticism, Gurudev has sung eloquent praises of *Nāmasmarana* making it absolutely clear that *Nāma* is God ( God in posse ), that *Nāma* is the symbol of the Divine carrying spiritual energy and that the process of *Nāmasmarana* is the process of identification with God.

b) When one considers Gurudev's devotion, love and respect as well as his gratitude towards his Guru, one is reminded of Dnanadeva's commentary on आचार्योपासना in B. G. 13-7 in Dnaneshwari. It is said that a devotee attains liberation by developing intensely any one emotion about God. When I asked Gurudev, " which particular feeling about God or relationship with Him should one prefer ? " he said " The devotee should regard God as his Guru. This relationship between the devotee and his God-this intense emotion-is the best ". Gurudev always looked upon his Guru as God incarnate. To look upon one's Guru as God and to regard God as one's Guru are practically the two sides of the same coin. I cannot help feeling that only on account of his incomparable devotion to his own Guru he gave this reply to my question.

c) Once he mentioned two very significant points regarding the Guru's function towards his disciple. (i) The

mother feeds the foetus in the womb through the anbilical Chord. In the same way, the Guru spiritually feeds his disciple through *Nāma*. I remember another occasion even more significant than this. In the year 1936, a certain professor had come to Nimbal and he and I were talking to Gurudev. After some time, the Professor left and then Gurudev said to me, "Just as the mother nourishes her baby with her milk, the Guru also nourishes his disciple spiritually with his spiritual power. This is an actual experience, Ganpatrao. What greater authority can there be than experience? In the past I did not impart *Nāma* or initiate *Sādhaks* and so I could not experience this. But, when I started initiating aspirants I began to experience this." Towards the end of 1920 Gurudev attained the spiritual height necessary for initiating others. But as long as his senior *Gurubandhu*, Sri Amburao Maharaj alias Baba, was living, he refrained from imparting *Nāma*. It was only after the demise of Sree Baba in December 1933 that Gurudev started initiating others. This incident among reflects his extreme humility and modesty.

d) Gurudev very rarely spoke about his experiences or about his spiritual height. Others too did not generally dare to ask him about it. Nevertheless, he expressed his self-confidence occasionally, especially in the company of two or three intimate associates. In this respect, the following incidents would he found significant:—

i) Gurudev could easily read the character of a man immediately on seeing him. I had been observing this since 1913. So I once asked him, "How can you know this?" Thereupon he replied with a smile "Ganpatrao, should one not come to know even this much after practising *Nāma* for such a long time?."

ii) As has been said above, Gurudev attained the

spiritual heights necessary for initiating others towards the end of 1920. Even then he did not start initiation till 1934. Once, he appeared to have been somewhat perturbed, probably because some one had made an improper remark about this matter. Without directly referring to the person and the remark concerned, Gurudev said to me, when we were alone, "The authority to initiate has not to be given by another person. In fact, nobody is capable of giving it. The aspirant concerned knows for himself if he is worthy of initiating; and when one attains that authority no permission is necessary from any one."

e) Once I asked Gurudev, "What is your mental condition when your meditation reaches its highest pitch"? He replied, "*Nāma*, different sounds and colours and lights as well as forms and bliss are all fused together so completely that it is impossible to experience them separately in this state. Believe me, Ganpatrao, believe me, even when two hours pass in this state, one feels as if only ten minutes have passed " On all these three occasions there was no third person present.

f) Since the time I came into contact with him I could easily experience his extreme humility, his sympathy and compassion, his readiness to help others and indeed all those qualities mentioned in B. G. 7-11. My reverence towards him was the result of these virtues in him and it went on increasing as time passed. For, his *Sādhana* and spiritual experiences grew rapidly and side by side there was growth of these virtues. In fact, these virtues were the visible signs of his God-realisation. Indeed, Gurudev was born with natural qualities very favourable to his God-realisation, and therefore, on account of his spiritual tendency, these virtues were seen in his life right from the beginning. In this respect one is reminded of the following lines from the 18th Chapter of Dnyaneshwari regarding Sattwic knowledge -

तयापरी जया ज्ञाना । शिवादि तृणावसाना । इया भूतव्यवित
भिन्ना । नाडळती ॥ आरिसा पाहू जाता कोडे । जैसे पाहतेचि पाहिजे
पुढे । तैसे ज्ञेय लोटोनि पडे । ज्ञाताचि जै ॥ पुढे तेचि सात्त्विक ज्ञान ।
जे मोक्षलक्ष्मीचे भुवन ( ज्ञा. अ. १८, ५३३, ३६ व ३७).

This attitude of non-differentiation, i. e. of looking
upon others as oneself, culminated into the unitive experience
of seeing Brahman everywhere, as a result of his long and
dedicated *Sādhuna* and he attained the rare state of ‘ सर्वं
खल्विदं ब्रम्ह. ’ This state naturally perfected all his virtues
like अमानित्व.

g) I propose to mention two or three letters of Gurudev
that bear out the truth of the saying ‘ सहज बोलणे हित उपदेश ’
( Even a casual talk is valuable advice. ) How can I do justice
to what an ordinary person like myself saw in the brilliant life
of this Philosopher-Saint during the long contact of nearly 50
years ?.

i) When I got my M. A. degree, I said to Gurudev in
1914, “ I have to discharge some family responsibilities. If I
get a fairly well-paid job, I shall be able to discharge these
properly. In 1915 I secured a post of the Superintendent of Post
Offices. I wrote to Gurudev about this good news In his reply
of congratulations he wrote ” God fulfils all our pious wishes—
‘ सत्यसकल्पाचा दाता भगवान्. ’ In this reply was implied the
gentle warning of keeping one's desires meritorious.

ii) In 1915, when I was a Professor at Ajmer, there
was some small growth in my spiritual experience and I wrote
to him about this. He wrote back, “ Strike the iron while it
is hot ”.

iii) Sometimes he gave me a stern warning, of course

out of affection. In a letter or two I had mentioned some grandiloquent thoughts. He wrote in reply "Do not entertain morbid ideals which you can never attain."

iv) In 1942, when I was Deputy Post Master General at Lahore, Gurudev wrote to me "I remember you often and in my meditations." I could not understand his intention, but I cannot describe the great satisfaction I felt on reading the letter.

h) Once, while I was walking with Gurudev, he said as if to himself, "Maharaj had become one with the universe. How bitterly Nature must have mourned when Maharaj passed away". I did not grasp the meaning of these words. But they went deep down into my heart.

NOTE

# “ गुरुदेव को जेसा मैंने देखा ”

( गिरीश चन्द्र शर्मा )

मनोज्ञमधुराचाराः प्रियपेशलवादिनः

विवेचितारः कार्याणां निर्णेतारः क्षणादपिः (योगवसिष्ठ)।

महात्मा रानडे मनोज्ञ थे. अपने और पराये मन को जानने वाले थे. (मनः + ज्ञ) मन के ज्ञाता अर्थात् ' साक्षी चेता केवलो निर्गुणश्च' परम ज्ञानवान थे. प्रिय और मधुरभाषी थे. कार्यों का विषद रूप से विवेचन करने वाले थे. और क्षण में ही निर्णय कर लेते थे. वे संस्कृत, ग्रीक, इंग्लिश, हिन्दी, मराठी, कन्नड़ आदि भाषाओं के कितने विद्वान थे यह मेरे अनुमान के बाहर की बात है. उनका बाह्य आचरण कितना मधुर था उसके कुछ संस्मरण लिखता हैं.

अबसे लगभग 29 वर्ष पहले की बात है. जनवरी 1948 में उनसे मिला था. करीब 15 दिन उनकी आज्ञानुसार अध्यात्म विदयामंदिर में ठहरा था. मिलने का समय रात को सात बजे निश्चित हुआ था. मैं वहाँ श्री प्रकाश चंद्र गौतम एडम्बोकेट इलाहाबाद हाईकोर्ट के साथ जिस कमरे में उनकी बैठक होती थी, पहुँचा था. कमरे में केवल फर्श बिछा था. एक ओर श्री गुरुदेव बैठे थे, सामने कुछ विद्यार्थी बैठे थे. सभी विद्वान थे. उनमें से एक श्री प्रल्हाद कुलकर्णी थे. मैंने घूमते ही भूमि पर सिर रखकर प्रणाम किया. उन्होंने अपने पास बठने को कहा. मेरा उनका पहले से कोई परिचय नहीं था. उन्होंने पूछा

‘Who are you?’, मैने उन्हें याद दिलाई कि एक वार कैप्टेन परमात्मा शरण गौतम आपके पास आये थे. उन्होंने मेरा एक गीत गाया था ‘कोई लाख भुलाना चाहे मैं कूटस्थ न भूल जाऊंगा’. इस पर आपनें कहा था ‘Oh! It is a revolution in Vedanta. Who has written it? Send him to me.’ उनको तुरंत याद आ गई और बोले ‘Yes, yes’. फिर उन्होंने पूछा ‘Do you sing?’ मैने कहा ‘Yes, Sir, I do sing.’ उन्होंने कहा ‘गाओ’. मैने तुरंत एक कबीर दास का भजन ताली और चुटकी वजा वजाकर गाना आरंभ किया. ‘साधौ सहज समाधि भलो’. एक वार पूरा पद गाने के वाद फिर गाया, फिर गाया, वे सुनते सुनते अथाते नहीं थे. कई दिन तक गाता ही रहा — उस दरबार का मैं ही अकेला गायक था. फिर प्रश्नोत्तरों की झड़ी लगती थी. कभी वे मुझमे पूछते ‘Do you understand what you sing?’ कभी कभी मैं ‘yes’ कह देता तो मुझे विवेचन करना पड़ता. फिर वह उमका कुशलतापूर्वक विवेचन करते. कभी प्रेमोत्पत्त होकर कहते ‘Sharma! see.’ ‘बैठत उठत कवहुँ नहि छूटे ऐसी तारी लागी’, ‘आंखि न मूँद कान न रूंबू’ भक्तजन ध्यान दें. इस प्रकार वे कभी स्वयं, कभी मुझको ब्रह्मानंद, और भक्तिमाणर मे गोता लगवाते, कुछ पता नहीं रहता था कि कौन वे हैं औरकौन मैं हूँ. उस प्रत्यक्ष साक्षात् ब्रह्म के संस्मरण मेरे पास केवल भावावेश और आँसुओं की धार है.

‘भला हो तेरा ओ, रुला देने वाले
थमे आँसुओं को बहा देने वाले’

गुरुदेव के देखने का जहाँ तक प्रश्न है, ‘वह देखे जिसकी डोर लगी हो हरि से’ निर्गुण, — सगुण का भेद जिनका मिट चुका हो वे ही उनके मर्म को समझ सकते थे. परमार्थ सोपान नामक ग्रंथ का संकलन हो रहा था—प्रातः 7-11 व्रजे तक पहली बैठक, फिर 4-6 व्रजे सायं दूसरी, फिर रात 7 से 10 व्रजे तक तीसरी बैठक होती थी जिसमें

कभी कभी कालेजों के प्रोफेसर लोग भी आते थे – एक दिन हमारा समागम चल रहा था. मैं गाता था, बीच बीच मैं हमारा उनका संवाद चलता था. इसी बीच मैं प्रो. देवी दयाल शुक्ल, वार्डन हिन्दी होस्टल, मुझसे बोले “यह कैसे कहते हो? कभी सगुण से निर्गुण पर चले जाते हो तो निर्गुण से सगुण पर आ जाते हो”. इस प्रश्नपर प्रोफेसर रानडे और मैं हँस पड़े, फिर मैंने शुक्ल जी से कहा कि यह बात मैं नहीं बता सकता, आप प्रोफेसर रानडे से पूछिये तब वे उधर को सम्मुख हुए. फिर वे (गुरुदेव) करीब \frac{1}{2} घंटे तक उन्हें समझाते रहे. मैं जब कभी पद गायन, या दोहा, श्लोक आदि गाता, तो तुरंत वे पीछे बैठे विद्यार्थियों को निर्देश देते कि ‘Note down, part III, chapter V’ आदि. इस प्रकार हम सबका उपासना, विचार विमर्श, और सम्पादन का कार्य चलता रहता था. एक दिन डा. कौल ने मुझे बताया, देखिये हमारे गुरुदेव बहुत उच्च कोटि के महात्मा हैं. मगर लोग समझते नहीं हैं कि हमारे पूज्य गुरुदेव ने करीब 18 वर्ष से ‘अन्न नहीं खाया है, केवल चाय पर ही रहते हैं’. संत रानडे एक दोहा मुझसे बारबार कहते थे.

मनुआं मेरो मरि गयो, दुर्गल भयौ शरीर,
पीछे पीछे हरि फिरै, कहत कबीर कबीर ॥

वडे मुग्ध होकर मुझसे बार बार कहते ‘शर्मा ! पीछे पीछे हरि फिरैं कहत कबीर कबीर’. उस समय उनका मुख देखने लायक होता था – नूतन बालवत् भोलापन झलकता था. निमग्न हो जाते थे मानो कबीर का आवेश आ गया हो. उनका आचरण मधुर ही नही विचित्र भी था. हर मनुष्य को समझना कठिन था. मेरी समझ में: उनके लिये यह कहावत चरितार्थ होती है ‘वहि सर्वसमाचारा अन्त सर्वार्थशीतला:’ इसके अतिरिक्त स्थानाभाव के कारण अधिक नहीं लिखा जा सकता ! बहुत दिनों की घटना होने के कारण कुछ भूल हो गई हो, उनके लिये पाठक क्षमा करें.
